- [G-166] **[P2]** WASM Game Loading-State Async-Disposable Pattern — 2026 production pattern uses `IAsyncDisposable` / `[Symbol.asyncDispose]` / `await using` to wrap WASM game init (module fetch + GPU adapter + texture upload) ensuring deterministic cleanup on early-exit; prevents orphaned resources when player navigates away mid-init — source: https://blog.csdn.net/AlgoFun/article/details/160335021 (April 20 2026)

- [A-052] **[P3]** Safari 27 Apple-Intelligence Page Summarization on Minimal-Text Game Pages — AI-Generated Misleading Descriptions — Safari 27 AI summarizes page DOM text for tab/reader/spotlight; canvas-heavy GameZipper game pages have minimal extractable text and may get nonsensical/empty summaries ("a loading screen"); requires rich hidden descriptive `<section>` + meta + canvas aria-label — source: https://www.apple.com/macos/ (macOS 27 Golden Gate)
- [PWA-4] **[P2]** Safari 27 AI Tab Grouping Breaks PWA "Continue Playing" Single-Tab Session Assumption — AI tab grouping may clone/move a PWA tab, creating duplicate service-worker clients racing on the same IndexedDB game-state record; requires last-write-wins + BroadcastChannel sync for multi-client safety — source: https://so.html5.qq.com/page/real/search_news?docid=70000021_6676a2cb3ca28552 (June 13 2026)

- [P-98] **[P2]** WebGPU-vs-WebAssembly 256x256 Matrix Inflection-Point Dispatch — 72-matrix benchmark shows WASM FASTER than WebGPU at matrix sizes <= 256x256 (WebGPU 5-8x slower due to call-setup overhead), WebGPU 5-8x FASTER at >= 512x512; AI features must implement HYBRID DISPATCH (small -> WASM, large -> WebGPU) (WORKLOAD-SIZE-AWARE-PERFORMANCE-CROSSOVER-DISPATCH) — source: https://blog.csdn.net/weixin_29300931/article/details/159638655 (June 5 2026)
- [P-99] **[P2]** WebAssembly-Whisper INT8 Quantization + IndexedDB Cache Pattern — canonical pattern for in-browser speech-to-text: quantize model to INT8 (~100-300MB), fetch via HTTP Range, cache in IndexedDB (avoid repeat 100-300MB download), stream mic via getUserMedia; any future GameZipper voice feature MUST adopt this pattern with `navigator.storage.persist()` for cache survival (WASM-MODEL-QUANTIZATION-INDEXEDDB-CACHE-PATTERN) — source: https://blog.csdn.net/2501_93878564/article/details/154301431 (Nov 2025, recurring 2026)
- [A-051] **[P2]** MDN Mobile Accessibility Checklist — Authoritative 2026 Minimum Baseline — MDN's authoritative mobile-web-accessibility checklist: contrast >=4.5:1 normal text / >=3:1 large text; information conveyed via color must also be conveyed via text/icon; GameZipper should run Lighthouse a11y audit on every game page with min-score 90 (MDN-AUTHORITATIVE-MOBILE-ACCESSIBILITY-MINIMUM-BASELINE) — source: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/Accessibility/Guides/Mobile_accessibility_checklist (March 10 2026 update)

  - **[S-181] [P1]** CVE-2026-20805 Microsoft Desktop Window Manager (DWM) zero-day information-disclosure via remote ALPC interprocess channels exposing user-mode memory section addresses; patched Jan 13 2026 Patch Tuesday after in-the-wild exploitation (cybersecuritynews.com Jan 14 2026). OS-LEVEL-INFO-DISCLOSURE-VIA-INTERPROCESS-CHANNEL dimension; a compromised Windows host can escalate OUTSIDE the browser sandbox to read browser-process memory (cookies, localStorage gzFavs, session tokens). ## [v1.88.0] - 2026-06-22

### Added

  - **[B-125] [P2]** iOS Safari 26.x `position: fixed` bottom-gap (~10px above address bar) + top-fixed elements pushed under status bar during page scroll + address-bar auto-shrink (cloud.tencent.com/developer/article/2591937, current June 2026). BROWSER-FIXED-POSITION-SCROLL-ADDRESS-BAR-GAP dimension; affects GameZipper bottom-fixed `gz-ad-below-game` container, game-footer, and any `position: fixed; bottom: 0` HUD; workaround is `env(safe-area-inset-bottom)` + `dvh` units or inner-scroll-container restructure. Distinct from B-124 (Chrome desktop bookmark bar — different vendor/layer).
  - **[S-178] [P1]** Chrome weekly in-the-wild zero-day cadence — Infosecurity Magazine June 9 2026 reported another Chrome vulnerability exploited in the wild; 2025 retrospective (new.qq.com) documents 8 actively-exploited Chrome 0days averaging CVSS 8.5, all in CISA KEV. CHROME-WEEKLY-IN-WILD-ZERO-DAY-CADENCE-2026 dimension; GameZipper's "is current Chrome safe?" check must run WEEKLY; malicious ad iframe is the most likely delivery vector. Distinct from S-177 (single CVE) and W-185 (release schedule).
  - **[S-179] [P1]** Check Point critical auth-bypass bug exploited in-the-wild June 9 2026 (Infosecurity Magazine) — Check Point security gateways/firewalls widely deployed in corporate/school networks; a compromised gateway with an enterprise-trusted CA can MITM GameZipper HTTPS traffic and inject malicious JS without browser detection. NETWORK-SECURITY-GATEWAY-AUTH-BYPASS-IN-WILD-MITM-RISK dimension; GameZipper HTTPS+HSTS does NOT protect against enterprise-CA MITM; requires SRI hashes + CSP nonces + runtime integrity checks. Distinct from S-178 (browser-client) and W-187 (reachability).
  - **[S-180] [P2]** GlassWorm malware infrastructure takedown May 27 2026 (CrowdStrike + Google + Shadowserver, The Hacker News) — disrupts active infrastructure but triggers a 30-90 day COPYCAT SURGE as smaller actors replicate the now-public attack playbook (invisible-Unicode source-code hiding per S-124). SUPPLY-CHAIN-ATTACK-INFRASTRUCTURE-TAKEDOWN-RESIDUAL-COPYCAT-SURGE dimension; GameZipper npm/PyPI dependency scanning must increase to DAILY for 90 days post-takedown; residual IOCs persist on already-infected dev machines. Distinct from S-124 (malware discovery) and S-105 (bypass variant).
  - **[W-196] [P3]** iOS 26.3 / iPadOS 26.3 beta Continuity Camera + Sidecar regression (Jan 29 2026, IT之家) — wireless iPhone camera and Mac→iPad screen extension both broken in beta; CROSS-DEVICE-FEATURE-REGRESSION-DURING-OS-BETA-CYCLE dimension; GameZipper QA relying on Continuity Camera (screenshots, QuickTime capture) will fail during iOS beta cycles; WebRTC `getUserMedia` camera games may show "camera unavailable" on Mac via the broken Continuity bridge. Distinct from B-119 (stable release) and B-111 (new feature).
  - **[W-197] [P3]** phpBB critical flaw June 9 2026 (Infosecurity Magazine) — legacy PHP forum software still powering thousands of gaming communities; LEGACY-FORUM-SOFTWARE-CRITICAL-FLAW-2026 dimension; credential-theft from compromised forums enables account-takeover via password reuse on GameZipper (if accounts are added); if GameZipper adds a forum, use Discourse/Flarum not phpBB; enforce HaveIBeenPwned password checks. Distinct from S-164 (enterprise email) and S-166 (web server).
  - **[G-155] [P2]** 2025 China game grey-industry / black-market scaling parallel to legitimate market — FairGuard annual report Jan 8 2026: market hit 350.789B RMB (+7.68% YoY) / 683M users (+1.35% YoY) historic highs while grey-industry (cheats, bots, account trading, fake-charge scams) scaled in parallel with AI-assisted cheat generation. EMERGING-MARKET-GREY-INDUSTRY-SCALING-PARALLEL-TO-LEGITIMATE-GAMES dimension; GameZipper must validate scores server-side, rate-limit rewarded-ad rewards against bot-farming, and assume adversarial users. Distinct from S-058 (ad-fraud bots) and G-145 (retention).
  - **[C-130] [P3]** iOS App Store IAP payment-failure investigation pattern 2026 (April 28 2026, CN article) — "拉起苹果支付失败"/"支付受限" errors cluster into three root causes: network environment (unstable Wi-Fi, cellular, regional Apple-gateway restrictions), account information (outdated payment method, region mismatch, account flags), and payment method (expired cards, insufficient funds, bank declines). MONETIZATION-IAP-PAYMENT-FAILURE-INVESTIGATION-PATTERN dimension; defines the customer-support playbook for any future GameZipper IAP and the diagnostic flow for rewarded-ad load/callback failures; "known payment issues by region" help page needed for sanctioned/unreliable regions. Distinct from S-037 (publisher ad payment) and G-142 (monetization model).

## [v1.87.0] - 2026-06-22

### Added
- 10 new test cases from R206 Dynamic Test Intelligence cron industry research:
  - **[S-177] [P0]** Chrome Dawn WebGPU use-after-free CVE-2026-5281 — actively exploited in the wild (Google confirmed April 2 2026; discovered March 10 2026; patched Chrome 149.0.7827.114+). DAWN-WebGPU-UAF-IN-THE-WILD-2026 dimension; any GameZipper WebGPU game + third-party ad iframe is a candidate attack surface on unpatched Chrome <149.0.7827.114; GPUDevice.lost recovery does NOT protect against UAF (freed memory reused before event fires). Distinct from S-108 (npm supply chain) and P-060 (academic research).
  - **[S-176] [P1]** Chrome libvpx VP8/VP9 heap buffer overflow CVE-2026-1861 — malformed video stream RCE (patched Feb 4-5 2026). MEDIA-DECODER-HEAP-OVERFLOW-VIA-MALFORMED-VIDEO dimension; the rewarded-video ad path (Monetag/AdSense third-party video creatives) is the highest-risk surface; craft malformed VP9 → corrupt adjacent heap → potential localStorage/session-token read. Distinct from S-061 (WebCodecs JS API — this is the underlying native libvpx codec).
  - **[B-123] [P2]** Microsoft Edge sideload extension auto-cleanup — feature rolling out Nov 2025 auto-detects and removes malicious non-store sideloaded extensions. BROWSER-NATIVE-SIDELOAD-EXTENSION-AUTO-ENFORCEMENT dimension; QA-test-harness extensions installed via developer mode may be auto-quarantined mid-run causing flaky false-failures; any future GameZipper browser extension MUST ship via Edge Add-ons store. Distinct from W-151 (MV2 kill — that is API model, this is install-source).
  - **[B-124] [P3]** Chrome 148 bookmark-bar reappearance on new-tab regression (reported May 12 2026) — bookmark bar re-shows despite Ctrl+Shift+B hide, shrinking effective viewport ~40px. BROWSER-UI-CHROME-VIEWPORT-INTRUSION dimension; breaks pixel-perfect screenshot-diff CI (golden vs capture mismatch); games using 100vh or position:fixed top:0 may letterbox or overlap. Distinct from B-082 (Safari compact tab — different vendor).
  - **[P-083] [P2]** GPU-driver-corruption browser-rendering crash graceful software-fallback baseline (2026 steamwebhelper field reports). GPU-DRIVER-HEALTH-RENDERING-CRASH-SOFTWARE-FALLBACK dimension; outdated/corrupted GPU driver is a leading cause of in-browser rendering-process crash affecting ALL Chromium browsers; GameZipper games must use getContext('webgl', {failIfMajorPerformanceCaveat:false}) + webglcontextlost recovery + SwiftShader detection to survive. Distinct from P-043 (perf comparison) and B-069 (Firefox-specific context loss).
  - **[C-128] [P2]** 2026 web-automation platform smart-element-recognition QA capability coverage matrix (Tencent Cloud June 11 2026). WEB-AUTOMATION-CAPABILITY-COVERAGE-MATRIX-2026 dimension; industry baseline requires smart recognition of HTML/JS/dynamic/HIDDEN elements + smart wait + 6 interaction classes (form submit, popup, iframe switch, file upload, file download, page navigation); GameZipper QA gaps likely in hidden-element and file-upload coverage. Distinct from C-084 (single capability) and C-087 (specific tool).
  - **[P-084] [P1]** Real-time multiplayer network-latency thresholds — 2026 competitive baseline <30ms RTT / <1% packet loss (MOBA/FPS article April 29 2026). REAL-TIME-MULTIPLAYER-NETWORK-LATENCY-THRESHOLD-2026 dimension; any GameZipper PvP/real-time feature needs a connection-quality indicator + WebSocket ack/retry; DevTools throttling (Slow 3G = 400ms/33% loss) is the QA test environment. Distinct from P-042 (WebSocket scale — this is per-connection quality).
  - **[P-085] [P3]** WebGPU HDR texture float32-filterable capability detection (LearnWebGPU June 3 2026 + W3C webgpu spec texture-format-caps). WEBGPU-HDR-FLOAT32-FILTERABLE-CAPABILITY-DETECTION dimension; 32-bit HDR textures require adapter.features.has('float32-filterable') check before request, else silent black canvas on entry-tier mobile GPUs; default to float16 (universally filterable) and opt-up. Distinct from P-050 (perf) and P-026 (API fallback — this is within-WebGPU feature-level fallback).
  - **[G-154] [P3]** 2026 UGC game peak-concurrency benchmark — 47.4 million simultaneous users record (deep analysis March 11 2026). UGC-PEAK-CONCURRENCY-SCALE-BENCHMARK-2026 dimension; defines the upper-bound load-test target for any future GameZipper UGC layer; Cloudflare edge caching absorbs read load, only write path needs origin capacity; 2025 "reality check" warns UGC scale ≠ UGC revenue. Distinct from G-149 (monetization scale — this is concurrency scale).
  - **[C-129] [P2]** Unity-WebGL-export mobile-browser unsupported-warning audit (Unity 2020.1 docs, current 2026). UNITY-WEBGL-EXPORT-MOBILE-UNSUPPORTED-WARNING dimension; Unity officially does NOT support mobile WebGL — shows dismissible warning + may OOM on entry-tier devices; GameZipper must inventory Unity-exported games and replace the warning with a branded "best on desktop" notice or mark desktop-only. Distinct from C-060 (Phaser) and G-130 (Godot — different engine).

SAFARI-26.5-CSP-BYPASS-SENSITIVE-INFO-LEAK dimension; an attacker-crafted page content defeats a correctly-deployed GameZipper CSP on unpatched Safari 26.4 and earlier — ad iframes (gz-ad-below-game) could read parent DOM state including gzFavs localStorage favorites and the ?issue=1 bug-report form
  - **[W-193] [P2]** iOS 27 / macOS 27 Safari Apple Intelligence — natural-language browser commands + AI auto-tab detection + content-change notifications + cross-device tab themes (WWDC26 June 9 2026). AI-NATIVE-BROWSER-NATURAL-LANGUAGE-NAVIGATION dimension; new re-engagement channel (user says "notify me when GameZipper adds new puzzle games" → OS notification); AI tab-grouping requires descriptive <title> tags; cross-device handoff requires instant-save/resume (G-152) to work across iPhone→Mac
  - **[C-126] [P2]** Interop 2025 cross-browser compatibility milestone — Apple WebKit team annual review (Feb 6 2026) shows Safari achieved the LARGEST compatibility gain of any browser. INTEROP-2025-CROSS-BROWSER-COMPATIBILITY-MILESTONE dimension; the multi-vendor (Apple/Google/Microsoft/Mozilla) joint initiative defines the canonical cross-browser test matrix GameZipper QA must align with; 2025 focus areas (iframes, URL APIs, WebSocket, WebRTC) overlap GameZipper stack — convergence lets GameZipper drop polyfills
  - **[S-174] [P1]** TA4922 Chinese cybercrime group European expansion — Proofpoint June 4 2026 reports TA4922 now conducts more unique campaigns than any other cybercrime actor and expanded into Europe with new malware. CYBERCRIME-ACTOR-EUROPEAN-EXPANSION-2026 dimension; TA4922 lures use game-crack/cheat/mod themes — same channels game players use legitimately; GameZipper EU users now in direct blast radius; reputational risk if TA4922 impersonates GameZipper
  - **[S-175] [P1]** AI-powered ransomware toolkit automation (cybersecurity-help.cz June 3 2026) — ransomware kits now use AI for target selection (LinkedIn scraping), payload customization, AI-negotiated ransom. AI-AUTOMATED-RANSOMWARE-AS-A-SERVICE-2026 dimension; lowered attacker skill floor; GameZipper CI/CD pipeline (GitHub Actions + Cloudflare) is a higher-value target than user endpoints; git history + CDN cache provide ransomware-resistant backup posture
  - **[C-127] [P3]** Syncpack monorepo dependency-version consistency tool (JavaScript Weekly #16, ~April 2026) — used by Electron/Cloudflare/Vercel. MONOREPO-DEPENDENCY-VERSION-CONSISTENCY-AUTOMATION dimension; validates the "version drift = bug source" principle for GameZipper's 280+ game "monorepo" where each game includes shared scripts (monetag-manager.js, game-footer.js, games-data.js); inspires a GameZipper-specific shared-script-cache-bust drift checker
  - **[P-082] [P3]** Rolldown 1.0 Rust-based JS bundler — 10-30x faster than Rollup, becomes Vite 8 backbone (JavaScript Weekly #20, ~May 2026). RUST-NATIVE-BUNDLER-PERFORMANCE-10X-30X dimension; BUILD-PIPELINE-PERF dimension (distinct from P-077 runtime / P-081 render); future GameZipper build pipeline can adopt Vite 8 + Rolldown for 10x faster dev iteration on a 280-game monorepo
  - **[W-194] [P2]** Node.js 26.0.0 ships Temporal API enabled by default + V8 14.6 + Undici 8 (JavaScript Weekly #19, ~May 2026). TEMPORAL-API-DEFAULT-ENABLED dimension; SERVER-SIDE date-time API (distinct from past W entries which are browser-side); replaces bug-prone Date object; GameZipper server-side tooling (cron jobs, BI dashboard, analytics ETL) using new Date() at risk of timezone/DST bugs that Temporal fixes; the Dynamic Test Intelligence cron's 4-hour cadence must be computed in UTC (Temporal.Instant) to survive DST transitions
  - **[W-195] **[P3]** Safari Technology Preview 10-year anniversary (March 31 2026). APPLE-TECHNICAL-PREVIEW-10-YEAR-META-TESTING-PROCESS dimension; STP is the 2-week-cadence pre-release Safari channel that ships WebKit features 6-12 months before stable — GameZipper QA subscribing to STP catches Safari regressions early; STP is Mac-only (iOS Safari regressions need TestFlight); 10-year continuity proves Apple's commitment to the channel

- 10 new test cases from R205 Dynamic Test Intelligence cron industry research:
  - **[B-121] [P1]** Safari 26.4 WebKit regression sweep — 191 bugs fixed + 44 new features + 1 feature deprecation (March 24 2026). At this scale Safari 26.4 is functionally a new browser engine; load-bearing "bugs" Apple fixed may break games that depended on the old behavior. SAFARI-26.4-MAJOR-RELEASE-REGRESSION-SWEEP dimension requiring visual-regression baselines captured on 26.3 vs 26.4
  - **[P-080] [P1]** iOS WebKit engine monopoly performance penalty 28.6% — Microsoft Speedometer 3.1 benchmark (June 18 2026) shows Chromium-with-Microsoft-engine scores 28.6% higher than Safari on iOS; all iOS browsers forced to use Apple WebKit per App Store policy. IOS-WEBKIT-ENGINE-MONOPOLY-PERFORMANCE-PENALTY dimension — GameZipper iOS users hit a 28.6% lower performance ceiling than equivalent Android hardware
  - **[W-190] [P2]** Chrome 149 CSS Gap Decorations (column-rule / row-rule / column-rule-inset / row-rule-inset / column-rule-visibility-items / row-rule-visibility-items) shipped June 2 2026 — CHROME-149-CSS-GAP-DECORATIONS-NEW-FEATURE-ADOPTION dimension; progressive enhancement required (only Chrome 149+ supports it as of June 2026) with border/pseudo-element fallback for Firefox/Safari
  - **[W-191] [P2]** Chrome 148 AI-driven autofill + broader HTTP/3 support (May 7 2026) — CHROME-148-AI-AUTOFILL-HTTP3-WIDER-SUPPORT dimension; AI autofill must not mis-trigger on game text-input fields; HTTP/3 connection migration benefits mobile users switching WiFi/cellular mid-game
  - **[S-172] [P1]** AI-driven API-scale attack + AI Agent identity impersonation 2026 — IBM X-Force Threat Intelligence Index 2026 (March 3) + Check Point 2026 Cybersecurity Report (March 26) document 70% of orgs using compound AI, ~2000 attacks/org/week, AI Agent identity spoofing, API-scale attacks, AI browser black-box risks; security paradigm shifts from boundary defense to trust reconstruction. AI-DRIVEN-ATTACK-AGENT-IMPERSONATION-API-SCALE-2026 dimension
  - **[S-173] [P2]** Browser fingerprinting evolution 2026 — Canvas/WebGL/Audio/font multi-dimensional identity system replacing cookies under privacy regulations; users remain identifiable even after clearing all cookies + incognito.   - **[P-081] [P3]** BrowserQuest Canvas optimization pattern — dirty-rectangle + layered (3-canvas) rendering reference (March 23 2026 CSDN). CANVAS-DIRTY-RECTANGLE-LAYERED-RENDERING-OPTIMIZATION-PATTERN dimension; highest-impact optimization for Canvas 2D games targeting the iOS WebKit engine (recovers the P-080 28.6% penalty by reducing per-frame work 10x)
  - **[C-125] [P2]** WebGL/Canvas cross-browser compatibility tracking via MDN Browser Compatibility Data (BCD) open-source project (May 24 2026 CSDN). BCD-COMPATIBILITY-TRACKING-AUTOMATION dimension; integrate BCD into build pipeline to auto-flag unsupported-API usage before runtime QA; weekly BCD-diff CI job alerts when APIs change status
  - **[W-192] [P2]** ChromeOS 148 certificate configuration system migration (May 26 2026) — preparing for ChromeOS 150 LTS; changes which root CAs are trusted and how revocation is checked. CHROMEOS-148-CERTIFICATE-CONFIG-MIGRATION dimension; GameZipper TLS cert (Let's Encrypt/Cloudflare) must still chain to a ChromeOS-148-trusted root; education-sector Chromebook users disproportionately affected
  - **[G-153] [P3]** GameDev.Land adaptive layout for Poki HTML5 games workshop (May 13 2026) — mobile-first responsive reference: viewport user-scalable=no, CSS aspect-ratio, orientationchange debounce, env(safe-area-inset-*), 44x44px touch targets, Poki SDK pattern. POKI-ADAPTIVE-LAYOUT-MOBILE-FIRST-RESPONSIVE-REFERENCE dimension; industry best practice for mobile HTML5 game layout + prerequisite for portal syndication

## [v1.84.0] - 2026-06-22

### Added
- 7 new test cases from R204 Dynamic Test Intelligence cron industry research:
  - **[W-189] [P2]** Microsoft Edge Google account login support (announced June 18 2026 for July 2026 rollout) — CROSS-VENDOR-IDENTITY-PROVIDER-FEDERATION dimension where Microsoft Edge will accept Google OAuth credentials, creating a new account-federation attack surface and requiring the QA test matrix to expand with Edge-with-Google-account as a distinct auth-context row
  - **[S-169] [P1]** ClickFix attack variant using cmdkey + regsvr32 fileless LOLBINs (April 29 2026) — SOCIAL-ENGINEERING-LOLBIN-FILELESS-BYPASS dimension where attackers chain two Microsoft-signed Windows-native binaries to drop remote payloads without writing any file to disk, bypassing PowerShell-centric EDR; distinct from S-123 (Win+R PowerShell self-typed)
  - **[S-170] [P1]** Microsoft threat-intel-reported ClickFix variant targeting Windows Terminal paste-and-run with Lumma credential stealer (surfaced Feb 2026, reported March 9 2026) — SOCIAL-ENGINEERING-TERMINAL-PASTE-EXECUTION dimension distinct from S-123/S-169 because it targets Windows Terminal, a developer-oriented app whose paste-and-run UX is not yet covered by general-purpose EDR policies
  - **[B-120] [P2]** Apple first-ever PRODUCTION DEPLOYMENT of background silent (Rapid Security Response) WebKit update for CVE-2026-20643 (March 20 2026, Thomas Espach discovery) — SILENT-UPDATE-MECHANISM-FIRST-PRODUCTION-USE dimension distinct from S-095 (capability announcement) because B-120 documents the first ever actual mass deployment, proving the mechanism silently changes Safari WebKit version UNDER users mid-session
  - **[S-171] [P2]** .xor ransomware family 2026 consumer-endpoint attack chain (May 14 2026 deep-dive) — CONSUMER-ENDPOINT-RANSOMWARE-FAMILY-TTP-2026 dimension distinct from past ransomware entries because S-171 targets consumer game-players via malicious game cracks/cheats/mods (the same download channels GameZipper users use for legitimate extensions)
  - **[C-124] [P3]** Playwright cross-browser (Chromium + Firefox + WebKit) parallel testing methodology baseline from Tencent Cloud June 22 2026 guide — PLAYWRIGHT-CROSS-BROWSER-QA-METHODOLOGY-BASELINE dimension; explicit three-browser parallel matrix closes the GameZipper Safari/Firefox automated-regression gap by running Safari-equivalent WebKit tests on Linux CI without macOS hardware
  - **[G-152] [P3]** 2026 office-worker fragmented-session casual game design pattern (June 10 2026 上班族手游 research) — FRAGMENTED-SESSION-OFFICE-WORKER-CASUAL-DESIGN-PATTERN dimension requiring sub-second state-preservation across arbitrary interruption points so users can close the tab when a meeting starts and resume the exact game state 1-2 hours later

Cross-browser baseline completion: Chrome 111+ + Firefox 152+ (older Safari still missing). The FIREFOX-152-GETANIMATIONS-PSEUDOELEMENT-API dimension distinct from B-116 (Firefox 152 stable ship — umbrella entry) because P-076 is the SPECIFIC Web-Animations-API surface change with its own regression/feature-detection implications, distinct from G-120 (canvas pixel-diff CI pipeline — pixel-level not API-level), and distinct from P-045 (WebGPU shader cold-start — WebGPU not Web Animations API). ## [v1.79.0] - 2026-06-21
### Added
- 5 new test cases from industry research (R199 Dynamic Test Intelligence cron)
- **S-158** [P1] CVE-2026-0755 gemini-mcp-tool CVSS 9.8 Critical RCE via OS command injection in `contribute.ts` execAsync() — the LEGITIMATE Google-Gemini integration npm package used by Claude Desktop MCP clients; attacker-controlled input concatenated into shell command without validation → arbitrary OS command execution. Affects ALL versions ≤ 1.1.2 (initial 1.0.0 included); patched in 1.1.3. The AI-MCP-CLIENT-INTEGRATION-PACKAGE-RCE dimension distinct from S-128 (OpenClaw ClawHub marketplace malware — malicious SKILL), S-156 (Vim modeline RCE — EDITOR default-config), S-157 (GhostClaw scoped-namespace typosquat — DECEPTIVE-NAMESPACE), and S-101 (AI-extension prompt injection — browser-extension layer) because S-158 is the LEGITIMATE-BUT-VULNERABLE package dimension — the user installs the CORRECT package name `gemini-mcp-tool` and the package itself has a CVE. GameZipper QA pipeline that uses Hermes/Claude Code subagents inherits the RCE on dev machines when a Gemini MCP server is configured. (blog.csdn.net/weixin_42376192/article/details/158097649 June 10 2026 + ZDI-26-021 / ZDI-CAN-27783)
- **S-159** [P1] CVE-2026-2178 xcode-mcp-server command injection with NO PATCHED VERSION (GitHub Advisory GHSA-84fx-pwf3-7777 March 6 2026 — r-huijts/xcode-mcp-server ≤ 1.0.3, advisory explicitly states "Patched versions: None"). The AI-MCP-SERVER-WITH-NO-PATCH-AVAILABLE dimension distinct from S-158 (gemini-mcp-tool HAS a patched version 1.1.3) and S-101 (AI-extension prompt injection — browser-extension layer not dev-tool CLI) because S-159 is the NO-PATCH-AVAILABLE dimension where the ONLY remediation is UNINSTALL — QA cannot "just upgrade" but must BLOCK the package from being installed at all. Traditional `npm audit --fix` guidance fails because `fixAvailable: false`. GameZipper dev toolchain that integrates Xcode via MCP (iOS testing automation, iOS Safari QA) inherits the RCE on macOS dev machines. (github.com/advisories/GHSA-84fx-pwf3-7777 March 6 2026)
- **W-182** [P2] CVE-2026-24061 GNU InetUtils telnetd USER environment variable authentication bypass (May 22 2026 disclosure — telnetd 1.9.3 to 2.7 fails to filter USER env var when calling /usr/bin/login, attacker injects `-f root` argument → bypass password check → root shell). One-line PoC: `USER='-f root' telnet -a TARGET`. The LEGACY-DAEMON-ENV-VAR-INJECTION-AUTH-BYPASS dimension distinct from W-162 (CVE-2026-32746 GNU InetUtils telnetd LINEMODE SLC OOB-write — MEMORY-CORRUPTION class in the SAME software product) because W-182 is the ENV-VAR-INJECTION-AUTH-BYPASS class — completely different vulnerability class in the same telnetd. The "same-product-different-class" pattern generalizes: a single daemon/library can accumulate multiple CVEs in DIFFERENT classes, and QA cannot stop at "we patched the latest CVE for product X". Affects GameZipper hosting-infra Linux servers with telnetd enabled and any in-house daemon that calls /usr/bin/login with user-controlled env. (blog.csdn.net/eidbsidbp/article/details/157291044 May 22 2026)
- **P-075** [P3] SteamOS 3.8.6 Beta first native AMD HDMI VRR support (May 30 2026) — V社 shipped SteamOS 3.8.6 Beta with experimental native HDMI VRR for HDMI-output Steam Deck / HTPC devices, AND AMD is integrating HDMI 2.1 features into the Linux mainline kernel AMDGPU driver (so future mainline kernels will ship HDMI VRR by default on all AMD-GPU Linux systems). The LINUX-OS-HDMI-VRR-MAINLINE-KERNEL-DRIVER-INTEGRATION dimension distinct from P-029 (high-refresh-rate 120Hz game phone rendering — mobile), P-055 (120Hz VRR game phone rendering — mobile), and P-063 (INP Chrome-DevTools web-perf metric) because P-075 is the LINUX-DESKTOP/HOME-CINEMA-OS VRR dimension affecting GameZipper hosting-infra stability (AMDGPU driver changes can introduce kernel regression taking GameZipper offline) AND player-side rendering on Steam Deck / SteamOS HTPC users (frame-pacing bugs hidden by fixed-60Hz vsync become user-visible judder on VRR displays). (new.qq.com/rain/a/20260530A04OOB00 May 30 2026)
- **C-120** [P3] macOS 27 Golden Gate super-wide 21:9 5K monitor support (June 10 2026) — macOS 27 extends high-resolution support to super-wide monitors (typically 21:9 aspect ratio, e.g., LG UltraFine 34", Dell UltraSharp 38", Samsung Odyssey G9 49"), allowing 5K-class resolution on super-wide displays. The SUPER-WIDE-ASPECT-RATIO-5K-RENDERING-BASELINE dimension distinct from B-112 (iOS 26 Liquid Glass over-transparency — OS-overlay), C-119 (Apple ImageCreator deprecation — framework removal), and W-155 (iOS 27/macOS Golden Gate stable-ship full-stack regression) because C-120 is the DISPLAY-ASPECT-RATIO-REGRESSION dimension — GameZipper games tested at 16:9 may have rendering bugs at 21:9 / 32:9 (layout breakage, canvas distortion from texture-size limits, ad-div horizontal stretching, footer-relative positioning errors). New "super-wide-display regression sweep" QA gate at viewport 5120×2160 (21:9 5K) and 7680×3240 (32:9 8K super-ultra-wide). (new.qq.com/rain/a/20260610A05NNV00 June 10 2026; apple.com/macos June 9 2026)

## [v1.78.0] - 2026-06-20
### Added
- 8 new test cases from industry research (R198 Dynamic Test Intelligence cron)
- **S-152** [P2] CVE-2026-34621 Adobe Acrobat / Acrobat Reader zero-day (CVSS 8.6) — exploit code appeared Nov 2025 in the wild, Adobe shipped fix mid-2026 after a 4+ month disclosure-lag window; PDF-as-malware-vector where players who open a "game manual PDF" or "newsletter PDF" attached to a malicious Monetag/AdSense creative get fully compromised. The PDF-MEDIA-VECTOR-DELAYED-DISCLOSURE-LONG-WINDOW dimension distinct from S-121 (npm Ghost campaign fake-install-log) because S-152 is the END-USER-SIDE PDF dimension not the developer-side npm dimension. (ithome.com/tag/lingriloudong/ IT之家 zero-day tracker — "Adobe 旗下 Acrobat DC、Reader DC 及Acrobat 2024 被曝存在一个零日漏洞(CVE-2026-34621),黑客通过构造恶意 PDF 文件即可远程植入恶意软件,完全控制系统。漏洞利用代码早在去年 11 月就已出现")
- **S-153** [P2] CVE-2026-21962 Oracle WebLogic Server Proxy Plug-in unauthenticated RCE (June 10 2026) — security-check-before-URL-decode ordering flaw → complete auth bypass + RCE + backend cluster penetration. The WEB-SERVER-PROXY-PLUGIN-UNAUTH-RCE-ORDERING-FLAW dimension distinct from W-163 (CVE-2026-21992 Oracle Identity Manager RCE — different Oracle product) and S-069 (HTTP/2 Rapid Reset DoS — different vuln class) because S-153 is the PROXY-PLUGIN-ORDERING-FLAW dimension. (blog.csdn.net/2302_79436907/article/details/159896100 June 10 2026 — "完全绕过身份认证: 攻击者无需任何凭证即可发起攻击" + "核心缺陷: 安全校验与URL解码的『顺序颠倒』")
- **S-154** [P2] CVE-2026-23918 Apache HTTP/2 mod_http2 Double-Free (May 6 2026 — single-version 2.4.66 only) — unauthenticated HEADERS + RST_STREAM frame pair → double-free → potential RCE. The WEB-SERVER-HTTP2-DOUBLE-FREE-LIBRARY-LEVEL dimension distinct from S-069 (HTTP/2 Rapid Reset DoS — different protocol-level vuln class) and S-086 (NGINX heap overflow — NGINX-specific not Apache) because S-154 is the APACHE-mod_http2-LIBRARY-LEVEL dimension. The SINGLE-VERSION-AFFECTED pattern is a NEW QA dimension: a regression in version N that affects ONLY version N (not N-1, not N+1) — a SPECIAL class of bug that cannot be caught by diff-based QA. (blog.csdn.net/weixin_42376192/article/details/161003983 May 12 2026 — discovered by Google security team)
- **S-155** [P2] CVE-2026-34926 Trend Micro Apex One path traversal + EDR-fleet hijack (May 21 2026 GHSA-4ccp-cqrh-3w9v, CISA KEV same-day May 21 2026, federal fix deadline June 4 2026) — pre-authenticated local attacker modifies key table → injects malicious code into auto-update channel → silently pushes malware to entire EDR-protected endpoint fleet. The ENDPOINT-PROTECTION-PLATFORM-COMPROMISE-VIA-AUTO-UPDATE-CHANNEL dimension distinct from S-074 (CSP tightening) and S-118 (DoubleClick RAT malspam) because S-155 is the SECURITY-PRODUCT-BECOMES-MALWARE-DISTRIBUTION dimension — the endpoint protection platform is itself turned into the attacker's distribution channel. (github.com/advisories/GHSA-4ccp-cqrh-3w9v May 21 2026; blog.csdn.net/weixin_42376192/article/details/161357281 May 24 2026 — "将 EDR (终端检测与响应) 系统变成自己的恶意软件分发平台")
- **S-156** [P1] CVE-2026-34714 Vim modeline default-config arbitrary command execution (CVSS 9.2) — tabpanel option missing P_MLE flag allows %{expr} injection WITHOUT enabling modelineexpr; autocmd_add() missing check_secure() bypasses sandbox → arbitrary OS command execution when victim opens a malicious file. The DEVELOPER-TOOL-DEFAULT-CONFIG-RCE dimension distinct from C-109 (Apifox desktop-client CDN poisoning — network-side dev-tool attack) and S-101 (AI extension — browser extension) because S-156 is the EDITOR-DEFAULT-CONFIG-MODELINE-EXEC dimension affecting any GameZipper dev who opens a seemingly-harmless text file. Affects Vim < 9.2.0272 on Linux/macOS/Windows. (blog.csdn.net/ximenjianxue/article/details/160021682 April 15 2026 — "漏洞等级: 高危, CVSS 9.2, 利用门槛极低, Vim 默认配置就能触发(不用改任何设置), 属于漏洞中的『核弹级』")
- **S-157** [P2] GhostClaw / @openclaw-ai/openclawai npm scoped-namespace typosquat (eSecurity Planet March 10 2026) — malicious npm package disguised as the OpenClaw installer, multi-stage infostealer + RAT stealing developer credentials, cryptocurrency wallets, and AI-CLI tokens. The AI-CLI-SCOPED-NPM-TYPOSQUAT-VIA-NAMESPACE-IMPERSONATION dimension distinct from S-128 (OpenClaw ClawHub marketplace malware — INSIDE the official marketplace) and S-129 (ClickFix macOS AppleScript delivery — social engineering) because S-157 is the SCOPED-NPM-NAMESPACE-TYPOSQUAT dimension where the attacker registers a deceptive scoped name (@openclaw-ai/) rather than the legitimate (@openclaw/) — a NEW vector in the AI-CLI impersonation family that bypasses character-level typosquat detectors. (esecurityplanet.com/threats/fake-openclaw-npm-package-installs-ghostclaw-malware March 10 2026)
- **B-115** [P2] CVE-2026-26176 Windows csc.sys Client-Side Caching driver TOCTOU privilege escalation (April 2026) — CscQueryDirectory function race condition (TOCTOU) allows unprivileged user → SYSTEM privilege escalation on Windows 11 26H2. The WINDOWS-DRIVER-TOCTOU-LPE dimension distinct from B-080 (CVE-2026-32202 Windows Shell spoofing CISA KEV — Shell UI not kernel-driver) and B-044 (Android June 2026 124-CVE bulletin — different OS) because B-115 is the OS-INTERNAL-DRIVER-LPE affecting Windows machines hosting browsers used by GameZipper players. (blog.csdn.net/oShuangYue12/article/details/160360940 June 16 2026)
- **P-074** [P2] CVE-2026-31431 "Copy Fail" Linux AF_ALG / splice() LPE (May 7 2026 Xint Code) — a 732-byte Python PoC achieves 100% reliable local privilege escalation on ALL Linux distributions with kernels built 2017 → patch date via a single 4-byte page-cache write chained through the authencesn logic flaw in AF_ALG + splice(). The BROAD-SCOPE-LINUX-LPE-AFFECTS-HOSTING-INFRA dimension distinct from B-115 (Windows-driver-LPE — different OS) and S-153 (WebLogic RCE — server-app-layer not kernel-layer) because P-074 is the KERNEL-LAYER-LPE dimension affecting the Linux hosting/CDN infrastructure serving GameZipper. The 9-YEAR-LATENT dimension (2017 → 2026) is a recurring pattern: similar latent LPE bugs likely exist in other kernel subsystems. (blog.csdn.net/safetybug/article/details/160644342 May 7 2026; xint.io/blog/copy-fail-linux-distributions May 7 2026 — PoC sha256: a567d09b15f6e4440e70c9f2aa8edec8ed59f53301952df05c719aa3911687f9; verified Ubuntu 24.04 LTS kernel 6.17.0-1007-aws + Amazon Linux)

## [v1.77.0] - 2026-06-20
### Added
- 7 new test cases from industry research (R197 Dynamic Test Intelligence cron)
- **S-150** [P1] CVE-2026-28962 Safari 26.5 WebKit CSP-bypass information disclosure (May 14 2026 Apple Safari 26.5 security list). The WEBKIT-CSP-BYPASS-INFORMATION-DISCLOSURE dimension distinct from S-138 (Safari 26.5 WebRTC process-crash fix — WebRTC subsystem from the SAME advisory) because S-150 is the CONTENT-SECURITY-POLICY dimension where malicious page content can circumvent the page-declared CSP and exfiltrate data the CSP should have blocked. GameZipper pages ship a Content-Security-Policy that protects users only if Safari/WebKit enforces it; on Safari < 26.5 any malicious Monetag/AdSense creative can exfiltrate cookies/localStorage/page DOM that the CSP should have blocked. The fix: "improving access restrictions, input validation, and processing logic" — a missing-check class of bug that may recur in future WebKit releases. (so.html5.qq.com/page/real/search_news?docid=70000021_0236a054d4370952 May 14 2026 IT之家 + Apple Safari 26.5 security list)
- **S-151** [P2] CVE-2026-26171 Microsoft .NET System.Security.Cryptography.Xml EncryptedXml uncontrolled-resource-consumption DoS (April 21 2026 Microsoft Security Advisory via PowerShell/Announcements issue #83). Affects PowerShell 7 < 7.6.1 and < 7.5.6; EncryptedXml class can be driven by attacker-crafted XML into unbounded resource consumption. The XML-CRYPTOGRAPHY-LIBRARY-DoS dimension distinct from prior CVEs because EncryptedXml is the XML-encryption primitive used in SAML/WS-Federation/SOAP-message-security/WS-Trust stacks — any future GameZipper backend or third-party-ad-server-side .NET component that decrypts XML-bearing payloads inherits the DoS. Pattern generalizes: parallel XML-crypto implementations in Java Apache Santuario, Python xmlsec, Go may have similar issues. PowerShell ships in many CI/CD environments — a CI runner that uses PowerShell to invoke XML parsing on attacker-controllable input can be DoS'd, blocking the build pipeline. (github.com/PowerShell/Announcements/issues/83 April 21 2026 + dotnet/runtime#126889)
- **W-181** [P2] WebKit Interop 2026 — 20 OFFICIAL cross-browser focus areas announced Feb 13 2026 by Apple WebKit jointly with Google Blink, Mozilla Gecko, Igalia (anchor positioning, advanced attr(), container style queries, contrast-color(), custom highlight, dialog/popover improvements, fetch upload + range requests, getAllRecords() for IndexedDB, JSPI for Wasm, media pseudo-classes, Navigation API, scoped custom-element registries, scroll-driven animations, scroll snapping, shape(), view transitions, web compat, WebRTC, WebTransport, CSS zoom). The OFFICIAL-MULTI-VENDOR-CROSS-BROWSER-COMPATIBILITY-BASELINE-2026 dimension distinct from W-150 (WASM 3.0 single-language features), W-154 (Chrome 150 single-browser), C-118 (Safari 27 single-vendor) because W-181 is the MULTI-VENDOR commitment that EVERY Chrome/Safari/Firefox release in 2026 must converge on — defining the 20 features whose cross-browser parity GameZipper games can rely on without per-browser polyfills. Continuously-updated dashboard at wpt.fyi/interop-2026. (new.qq.com/rain/a/20260213A015ZI00 Feb 13 2026 + WebKit blog)
- **B-114** [P1] iOS 27 device compatibility drop to iPhone 12+ (Macworld June 4 2026 + WWDC26 June 9 2026 keynote). iPhone 11, iPhone XR, iPhone XS, iPhone X and all earlier models are STUCK on iOS 26 (or earlier) for the REMAINING DEVICE LIFETIME. Apple's iPhone 6s 10-year-support precedent means iPhone 11 (released 2019) is on a support trajectory ending around 2029 — iOS 26 will remain the LATEST AVAILABLE Safari/WebKit version on iPhone 11 for years. The DEVICE-DROP-LONG-TAILED-STALE-WEBKIT-SURFACE dimension distinct from P-071 (12GB-RAM hardware gating for AI features WITHIN iOS 27) and W-155 (iOS 27 stable-ship regression sweep) because B-114 is the LONG-LIVED dimension where iPhone-11-and-earlier users never receive iOS 27+ patches, so any iOS 26 WebKit CVE remains exploitable on that sub-population for the device's lifetime. GameZipper must maintain an iOS-26-WebKit regression-test sweep IN PARALLEL with the iOS 27 sweep for YEARS. (macworld.com/article/1659017/ios-versions-list.html June 4 2026 + Macworld WWDC26 device-compatibility list)
- **C-119** [P3] Apple ImageCreator class deprecation in iOS 27 / iPadOS 27 / macOS 27 / visionOS 27 (June 11 2026 Apple Developer News). The original Image Playground framework entrypoint for on-device AI image generation is being DISCONTINUED. Apple's specific deprecation contract: beta OS releases — code still compiles with Xcode warnings but ImageCreator-using apps fail at runtime in TestFlight; public OS releases — code WILL NOT COMPILE. The FRAMEWORK-API-REMOVAL-SILENT-BREAKING-CHANGE dimension — the FIRST test case covering a HARD API REMOVAL with NO runtime shim. Distinct from prior deprecations (W-152 Edge Collections, W-151 MV2 hard kill) which involved REMOTE FEATURES being turned off; C-119 involves a LOCAL FRAMEWORK CLASS being removed at the COMPILE-TIME layer so the app BUILD FAILS. TestFlight-vs-Public-SDK asymmetry: a TestFlight build that "works" can fail in production because TestFlight uses beta SDK while public release requires the new SDK. (developer.apple.com/news/?id=08242015a June 11 2026)
- **P-073** [P3] WebGPU vs WebGL client-side AI inference benchmarks (SitePoint Feb 25 2026 — "WebGPU vs. WebGL: Performance Benchmarks for Client-Side Inference"). Running LLMs and vision models directly in the browser has shifted from novelty to genuine engineering goal. The WebGPU-vs-WebGL CLIENT-SIDE-AI-INFERENCE dimension distinct from P-067 (WebGPU+WASM shared-memory boundary — graphics/compute) and P-069 (WebGPU 39x draw-call throughput — pure-graphics metric) because P-073 is the AI-INFERENCE dimension — running neural-network forward passes for LLM token generation or vision-model classification on the client device. The WebGL fallback is required for B-114 long-tail devices (iPhone XR/XS/11, low-end Android) which lack WebGPU AND lack the RAM for client-side AI inference — the WebGL-fallback performance is the BASELINE that any future GameZipper AI feature must be designed for, not the WebGPU-native performance. (sitepoint.com/webgpu-vs-webgl-inference-benchmarks Feb 25 2026)
- **G-148** [P3] JavaScript Weekly 2026 Week 20 (cloud.tencent.com June 2026) — Node 26.1 experimental FFI support + Bun built-in headless-browser automation + cron scheduling + BlueJS AOT JS compiler (1.2MB binary, 5ms startup, 3.8MB peak memory) + Astro 6.3 experimental advanced routing + Valibot 1.4.0 TypeScript schema-validation library. The 2026-MIDYEAR-JS-RUNTIME-AND-TOOLING-EVOLUTION dimension distinct from W-159 (Rolldown 1.0 + Vite 8 build-toolchain migration — bundler-only) and C-110 (browser DevTools console CVE-scanner) because G-148 covers RUNTIME-FEATURE and TOOLING changes affecting future GameZipper build-pipeline choices — Node FFI enables native-library calls without Node addons; Bun's built-in browser automation is a direct competitor to current Kachilu/Playwright QA tooling; Astro 6.3 advanced routing could enable a future GameZipper SSG migration that eliminates the recurring games-data.js orphan-entry bug (5+ recurrences documented in post-deploy-verification skill). (cloud.tencent.com/developer/article/2679559 June 2026 JavaScript Weekly #20)

## [v1.76.0] - 2026-06-20
### Added
- 7 new test cases from industry research (R196 Dynamic Test Intelligence cron)
- **S-146** [P1] CVE-2026-32041 OpenClaw browser-control auth-bootstrap failure → unauthenticated continuation (March 2 2026 GHSA-vpj2-69hf-rppw GitHub Advisory CVSS HIGH). The AI-AGENT-FAILURE-MODE-CRITICAL-PRIVILEGE-CONTINUATION dimension distinct from S-128 (ClawHub marketplace malware — ACTIVE third-party skill) and S-129 (ClickFix macOS AppleScript delivery — social engineering) because S-146 is the PASSIVE-FAIL-OPEN-on-bootstrap-error dimension — even a fully-patched malware-free OpenClaw deployment would have been vulnerable because the bug lives in the auth-bootstrap code path, not in any skill; a local process or loopback-reachable SSRF path could access browser-control routes including evaluate-capable actions without auth. The fix: "Startup now fails closed" — bootstrap error causes startup failure rather than startup-without-auth. (github.com/advisories/GHSA-vpj2-69hf-rppw March 2 2026 official GitHub Advisory Database — explicit HIGH severity + "a local process (or a loopback-reachable SSRF path) could access browser-control routes, including evaluate-capable actions, without auth")
- **S-147** [P1] CVE-2026-25253 OpenClaw ClawJacked — URL-parameter WebSocket hijacking RCE (Jan 2026, CVSS 8.8 HIGH, 135,000+ public-exposed instances + 15,000+ at-RCE-risk per SecurityScorecard Mar 2026). The AI-AGENT-URL-PARAMETER-WEBSOCKET-HIJACKING-AUTH-TOKEN-LEAK dimension distinct from S-146 (PASSIVE auth-bootstrap fail-open) and S-141 (SANDWORM_MODE env-var-toggle runtime evasion) because S-147 chains THREE independent defects — unvalidated URL query param `gatewayUrl` persisted to localStorage + auto-trigger `connectGateway()` on lifecycle hook + WebSocket Origin-header validation gap — to produce a NO-CLICK RCE via single-malicious-link delivery; reported by depthfirst General Security Intelligence; CSDN called it "一键触发的远程代码执行攻击" (one-click RCE attack) where "攻击者仅需通过一个恶意链接即可完全控制受害者系统,无需任何用户交互". Affects OpenClaw < 1.8.1. GameZipper is an ATTACK VECTOR for OpenClaw compromise because a malicious Monetag/AdSense creative served on a GameZipper game page can compromise any visiting developer who has OpenClaw installed locally. (blog.csdn.net/FreeBuf_/article/details/157685273 Feb 3 2026 depthfirst write-up; blog.csdn.net/sd7o95o/article/details/158105132 May 16 2026 full CVE detail with code; blog.csdn.net/zhuimengkaifazhe/article/details/158975962 Mar 12 2026 SecurityScorecard 135K/15K/12% stats)
- **S-148** [P1] OpenClaw CVE cluster — CVE-2026-33573 (Mar 29 2026 workspace-boundary-bypass via agent RPC parameters) + CVE-2026-41370 (Apr 28 2026 path-traversal via inbound-channel attachment path in ACP dispatch) — both HIGH CVSS. The AI-AGENT-VULNERABILITY-CLUSTER-ACCELERATION dimension distinct from prior OpenClaw entries (S-128 marketplace, S-146 bootstrap-fail, S-147 WS-hijack) because S-148 documents the META-PATTERN — a single open-source AI-agent platform at the OPERATING-SYSTEM-FOR-AGENTS layer (which Hermes, OpenClaw, PilotDeck W-179 all are) accumulates severe CVEs at a rate that dwarfs traditional single-CVE-per-product browser/library CVE cadence. Each of the 4 CVEs has a DISTINCT ROOT CAUSE (URL-param + auth-bootstrap + RPC-boundary + path-traversal). The 4 root causes are the 4 most common agent-platform vulnerability classes — GameZipper must audit any future Hermes/OpenClaw/PilotDeck tool against ALL FOUR classes before deployment. (github.com/advisories/GHSA-5w3r-prr4-7j25 Mar 29 2026 CVE-2026-33573; github.com/advisories/GHSA-pmg8-9xxh-v2wv Apr 28 2026 CVE-2026-41370; vulncheck.com advisories)
- **S-149** [P2] Mozilla + Anthropic Mythos Preview = 271 Firefox bugs in 2 months (180 high-severity + 80 medium + 11 low); Mozilla DIRECTLY published a confirmation blog post May 8 2026 to address "AI 找 Bug 质疑" (AI-found-bug skepticism). The AI-DISCOVERY-VOLUME-VENDOR-DIRECTLY-CORROBORATED-FIREFOX-SIDE dimension distinct from S-113 (Mythos 100 Chromium zero-days in 15 days — Chromium-side, defensive disclosure) because S-149 is the FIREFOX-SIDE vendor-confirmed corroboration that AI-discovery volume is REAL not hallucinated — the strongest possible evidence. The 66% high-severity ratio (180/271) means MOST AI-found bugs are exploitation-reachable via normal browsing — GameZipper Firefox regression sweep must run WEEKLY not monthly. (so.html5.qq.com/page/real/search_news?docid=70000021_53769fd53ba77252 May 8 2026 Mozilla blog + 财联社 reporting)
- **W-180** [P2] Anthropic Claude Fable 5 + Mythos 5 first PUBLIC GENERAL-AVAILABILITY Mythos-class model release (June 9 2026, SWE-bench Pro 80.3% vs Opus 4.6 53.4%, 1M token context, $10/$50 per MTok pricing). Fable 5 = Mythos 5's safety-aligned version for general public; Mythos 5 = full capability for trusted cybersecurity research partners. The AI-VULN-GENERATION-CAPABILITY-MADE-PUBLICLY-AVAILABLE dimension distinct from C-114 (Mythos vuln-GENERATION capability announcement — INTERNAL-only confirmation) because W-180 documents the OPPOSITE DECISION — Anthropic DID release a Mythos-class model to the public, with safety guardrails that are CONFIGURATION-TIME not CAPABILITY-TIME and can in principle be bypassed via prompt-injection or jailbreak. Anyone with $10 can now invoke a Mythos-tier model to generate phishing UIs (C-116), exploit chains (C-114 offensive), or malware obfuscation that defeats existing GameZipper supply-chain scanners. The 1M-token context means Fable 5 can analyze the ENTIRE GameZipper codebase in a single context. (so.html5.qq.com/page/real/search_news?docid=70000021_9726a28dde799552 June 10 2026 IT之家; blog.csdn.net/msbcsdn/article/details/161860642 June 10 2026 SWE-bench Pro 80.3%; blog.csdn.net/nmdbbzcl/article/details/161870199 June 16 2026; cnblogs.com/aiwangjianguo/p/20549551 June 15 2026 1M context + $10/$50 pricing + 50M-line Ruby migration)
- **B-113** [P2] Apple MIE (Memory Integrity Enforcement) hardware memory safety deployed on M5 Mac + A19 iPhone (Feb 4 2026 Apple Platform Security Guide update). MIE was developed over 6+ months and validated against sophisticated spyware attacks; it CONSTRAINTS attacker ability to exploit memory-corruption vulnerabilities, providing PERSISTENT memory safety for kernel + critical attack surfaces. The HARDWARE-LEVEL-MEMORY-SAFETY-LAYER-FOR-BROWSER-GAMES dimension distinct from B-097 (iOS 26.5 advisory MENTIONS M5 bypass as one of 80+ vulns) because B-113 documents MIE INTRODUCTION as a NEW hardware-guarantee layer — distinct from B-097 which covers the BYPASS side. Any GameZipper browser-game JS/WASM code running on M5/A19 devices benefits from a hardware-level guarantee that classic memory-corruption exploit techniques are MUCH HARDER. MIE shifts attack economics toward non-MIE devices (M1-M4, A1-A18, Android). (new.qq.com/rain/a/20260204A063IK00 Feb 4 2026 Apple Platform Security Guide update)
- **P-072** [P2] Calif researchers used Claude Mythos Preview to break Apple M5 macOS kernel MIE in 5 days (work done April 2026, public disclosure May 17-21 2026). The AI-ASSISTED-HARDWARE-MEMORY-SAFETY-BYPASS-CONCRETE-PROOF-OF-CONCEPT dimension distinct from C-114 (Mythos capability announcement — INTERNAL-only) and B-113 (MIE introduction — defensive layer) because P-072 documents a CONCRETE PoC where Mythos Preview was used to defeat a SHIPPING HARDWARE-LEVEL DEFENSE that took 5 years + billions to build. Calif (researchers Bruce Dang, Dion Blazakis, Josh Maine) achieved the FIRST PUBLIC Apple M5 chip macOS kernel memory-corruption exploit using TWO CHAINED UNPATCHED BUGS to achieve unprivileged-local-user → root shell; they physically went to Apple HQ to deliver the report. The 5-day timeline means GameZipper must treat any memory-corruption-class bug in browser engine code (WebKit, Chromium V8, Skia, ANGLE) as a 5-DAY-TO-EXPLOIT risk on MIE-protected devices, not multi-year — the existing S-057 20h exploit-window SLA must be tightened. Trend: 5 years + billions for MIE; 5 days for Mythos Preview to break it; next MIE successor will likely fall in HOURS under Mythos 5. (blog.csdn.net/qq_73472828/article/details/161193885 May 21 2026 full write-up "Anthropic Claude 5 天攻破 Apple M5 macOS 内核漏洞"; jdon.com/92074-first-public-kernel-exploit-apple-m5-mythos-previe.html May 17 2026 极道 writeup)

## [v1.75.0] - 2026-06-20
### Added
- 6 new test cases from industry research (R195 Dynamic Test Intelligence cron)
- **S-144** [P2] CVE-2026-41008 Spring Security Authorization Server Open Redirect via request_uri (June 9 2026 spring.io/security/cve-2026-41008 MEDIUM CVSS AV:N/AC:L/PR:N/UI:R/S:C/C:L/I:L/A:N) — Spring Security Authorization Server's authorization endpoint performs insufficient validation of the `request_uri` parameter; an attacker can craft a malicious authorization request containing an invalid `request_uri` AND an arbitrary unvalidated `redirect_uri` that chains into an Open Redirect. OAUTH-PAR-OPEN-REDIRECT dimension (Pushed Authorization Request / RFC 9126) distinct from prior OAuth coverage because CVE-2026-41008 is the request_uri-side Open Redirect that affects any GameZipper OAuth flow delegating to a Spring Security backend (Google/Apple/Microsoft sign-in, Discord OAuth for leaderboards). Affects Spring Authorization Server 7.0.x (< 7.0.6) and 1.5.x (< 1.5.8); reported by Jon Kjennbakken of Vipps MobilePay. (spring.io/security/cve-2026-41008 June 9 2026 official advisory)
- **S-145** [P3] CVE-2026-2472 Google Cloud Vertex AI SDK stored XSS in `_genai/_evals_visualization.py` (Feb 20 2026 GCP-2026-011) — google-cloud-aiplatform versions 1.98.0 to (not including) 1.131.0 contain a Stored XSS in the eval-visualization module; any attacker-controlled markup in the eval payload executes as script in the page origin when the eval results render in a browser-trusted Jupyter/Dash page. AI-SDK-STORED-XSS-IN-EVALS-VISUALIZATION dimension distinct from C-113 vibe-coding (developer-side risk) and C-116 Gemini-generated phishing UI (model-side risk) because S-145 is the RUNTIME-side risk — an AI SDK rendering eval output in a browser is XSS-pwned by any eval payload containing attacker-controlled markup. Affects any future GameZipper AI feature that visualizes LLM evals. Discovered by Din Asotić, PoC by Joshua Provoste. (github.com/JoshuaProvoste/CVE-2026-2472-Vertex-AI-SDK-Google-Cloud Feb 20 2026 official CVE write-up + PoC)
- **B-112** [P1] iOS 26 Liquid Glass Control Center over-transparency regression (June 8 2026 tenorshare.tw + cnblogs user-adaptation logs) — iOS 26's default-on Liquid Glass design makes the Control Center over-transparent so the OS-level overlay visually merges with the underlying app content, causing users to confuse which UI layer they are tapping. IOS-26-LIQUID-GLASS-OS-LEVEL-VISIBILITY-REGRESSION dimension distinct from B-090 (Safari 27 525 fixes) and B-110 (China NVDB iOS WebKit red alert) because B-112 is the OS-OVERLAY-VISIBILITY-CLASH dimension — when a GameZipper player on iOS 26 pulls up the Control Center mid-game, the game canvas bleeds through the over-transparent Control Center, creating visual confusion and mis-taps. Affects ~20% of GameZipper mobile traffic on iOS Safari. Documented user complaint: "液體玻璃效果讓控制中心變得過於透明,導致它與主畫面融合並顯得雜亂" (Liquid Glass effect makes Control Center too transparent, causing it to merge with the home screen and look cluttered). Apple's only pre-iOS-27 remediation is for users to enable "Reduce Transparency" in Settings → Accessibility. (tenorshare.tw/ios-update-problems June 8 2026; cnblogs.com/jiushi8888/p/19246072 Nov 20 2025 iOS-26 adaptation log)
- **A-041** [P2] iOS 27 Liquid Glass transparency slider + auto-adapt to "Reduce Transparency"/"Increase Contrast" accessibility settings (WWDC26 June 11 2026) — Apple announced iOS 27 adds a CONTINUOUS transparency slider for Liquid Glass (ranging from "超清晰" super-clear to "完全着色" fully-tinted), replacing iOS 26's binary on/off. Liquid Glass now auto-adapts to OS accessibility preferences — when the user enables "Reduce Transparency" or "Increase Contrast", Liquid Glass automatically shifts toward the opaque end without manual slider adjustment. Third-party apps using Liquid Glass get the improvement WITHOUT recompiling. IOS-27-LIQUID-GLASS-TRANSPARENCY-SLIDER-A11Y-AUTO-ADAPT dimension distinct from B-112 (iOS 26 over-transparency regression — the PROBLEM) because A-041 is the SOLUTION Apple shipped in iOS 27; distinct from A-037 (iOS 27 Accessibility framework rewrite — API-level) because A-041 covers the visual-design-language accessibility adaptation. (so.html5.qq.com/page/real/search_news?docid=70000021_4876a2a514b51852 June 11 2026)
- **C-118** [P2] Safari 27 beta ship with 58 new features + customizable `<select>` + scroll anchoring + WebAssembly JSPI (June 9 2026 webkit.org "News from WWDC26: WebKit in Safari 27 beta") — Safari 27 beta shipped with 58 new features + 525 bug fixes (the largest Safari feature drop in years). GameZipper-relevant features: (a) Customizable `<select>` via `appearance: base-select` (CSS-native stylable select, no more hacky div-rebuild replacements); (b) Scroll Anchoring (`overflow-anchor`) so dynamically-inserted content above the viewport does not cause scroll jumps; (c) WebAssembly JSPI (JavaScript Promise Integration) — async WASM call ABI for compute-heavy game logic compiled to WASM. SAFARI-27-BETA-STABLE-MILESTONE-WEBKIT-FEATURES-COUNT dimension distinct from W-129 (Safari 27 AI tab organization — single feature) and B-090 (Safari 27 WWDC26 525 fixes — fix-count only) because C-118 covers the 58-NEW-FEATURES surface that needs NEW QA coverage. (webkit.org/blog June 9 2026; web-standards.dev June 9 2026 — explicit "58 new features, 525 fixes, customizable <select>, scroll anchoring, and WebAssembly JSPI"; webkit.org/blog June 12 2026 "Web technology sessions at WWDC26")
- **W-179** [P3] Tsinghua PilotDeck open-source Agent OS May 28 2026 (OpenBMB / THUNLP / ModelBest / AI9Stars, AGPL-3.0, TypeScript) — an Agent Operating System built around the "WorkSpace" concept with three distinguishing dimensions: (1) memory-whitebox-editable (locate the EXACT memory entry causing an agent mistake and edit directly, without restarting the chat); (2) per-task token tracking (token cost tracked per individual task, not per session, making background agent runs economically viable); (3) automatic model routing by difficulty (simple tasks route to cheaper models, complex to flagship). MEMORY-EDITABLE-AGENT-OS-WITH-PER-TASK-TOKEN-TRACKING-AND-MODEL-ROUTER dimension distinct from existing OpenClaw (S-128) / Anthropic Mythos (C-114, S-113) / SANDWORM_MODE (S-141) dimensions because W-179 is the BENIGN-CHINESE-ACADEMIC open-source agent OS dimension affecting QA-pipeline-economics + memory-debugging patterns. Relevant to GameZipper because the puzzle-pipeline uses Hermes/Claude Code subagents and PilotDeck-class per-task tracking + memory-editability would change how the recurring games-data.js orphan-entry bug is debugged. Project got 400+ stars in the first week. (github.com/OpenBMB/PilotDeck May 28 2026; cnblogs.com/itech/p/20199005 May 28 2026; blog.csdn.net/m0_75253087/article/details/161524933 June 9 2026)

## [v1.74.0] - 2026-06-20
### Added
- 6 new test cases from industry research (R194 Dynamic Test Intelligence cron)
- **W-176** [P2] Chrome 148 Android approximate-location permission toggle (May 7 2026 IT之家) — Chrome 148 Android shipped a NEW platform-level privacy setting: "Android 版新增了一项设置,允许网站使用近似位置而非精确位置" (Android added a setting allowing websites to use approximate location instead of precise location). APPROXIMATE-vs-PRECISE-LOCATION-PERMISSION-TOGGLE dimension distinct from S-103 (Privacy Sandbox killed — cross-site ad/analytics tracking cookies) because W-176 is the GRANULARITY-of-consented-geolocation dimension, not the cross-site-tracking-cookies dimension; distinct from B-081 (Chrome storage partitioning iframe ad cookies — partitions cookie storage, not geolocation accuracy). GameZipper's current 280+ catalog does not call navigator.geolocation, BUT any FUTURE geolocation-using game (geo-puzzle, weather-themed, location-leaderboard) must QA both the precise-permission and the new approximate-permission paths. Test: on Chrome Android 148+, grant APPROXIMATE only and verify the game does NOT crash, does NOT loop-retry, and does NOT silently fingerprint precise location from approximate + WiFi scan. (so.html5.qq.com/page/real/search_news?docid=70000021_83069fc56b987652 May 7 2026)
- **W-177** [P2] Apple App Store AI-Agent Marketplace integration (WWDC26 June 9 2026 keynote + The Information pre-leak June 5 2026) — Apple plans to integrate AI agents (智能体) into the App Store as a first-party distribution surface allowing users to delegate booking reservations, daily-affairs management, document editing, and smart-home control to AI agents downloaded from the App Store. APPLE-FIRST-PARTY-AI-AGENT-MARKETPLACE dimension distinct from S-128 (OpenClaw ClawHub AI-agent-marketplace supply-chain — a MALICIOUS third-party marketplace) because W-177 is Apple's BENIGN-FIRST-PARTY AI-agent store that nonetheless expands the AI-agent-as-distribution-channel surface any future GameZipper iOS app or PWA wrapper must compete with; distinct from B-108 (iOS 27 Siri AI standalone app — Siri as a single first-party chatbot) because W-177 is a MARKETPLACE of third-party-vendored agents — a distribution channel, not a single app; distinct from W-164 (ChatGPT 2026 sponsored-content / AI-advertising — paid placement in AI answers) because W-177 covers action-taking agents that interact with user data and external services. GameZipper future iOS app or PWA wrapper installable via App Store faces a discovery-competition surface where players may invoke AI agents to find games; GameZipper must ensure schema.org VideoGame metadata is well-formed for AI-agent extraction. (so.html5.qq.com/page/real/search_news?docid=70000021_8716a2269eb24452 June 5 2026; so.html5.qq.com/page/real/search_news?docid=70000021_2706a2207c793752 June 5 2026)
- **C-116** [P2] Gemini 3.5 Flash generates interactive web UI (Google I/O May 20 2026) — Google I/O 2026 announced Gemini 3.5 Flash with capability to generate "更丰富、更具交互性的网页用户界面与图形" (richer, more interactive web user interfaces and graphics). AI-GENERATED-INTERACTIVE-WEB-UI-FROM-PROMPT dimension distinct from C-095 (HTML-in-Canvas API — a Chrome I/O 2026 RENDERING API, not a model capability) because C-116 is a MODEL CAPABILITY that takes a natural-language prompt and produces a working interactive HTML+CSS+JS UI; distinct from C-113 (vibe coding — human-curated AI code) because C-116 covers end-user-facing LLM-generated UI where an attacker can prompt the LLM to produce a phishing UI indistinguishable from a legitimate GameZipper page; distinct from W-164 (ChatGPT sponsored-content — paid placement) because C-116 covers the underlying CAPABILITY that enables the phishing-clone vector. GameZipper anti-phishing pipeline must extend to LLM-generated interactive clones; periodic adversarial prompts to Gemini 3.5 Flash for "create a login page for gamezipper.com" must be detected. CSP + Trusted Types must block typical LLM-phishing exfiltration patterns. (so.html5.qq.com/page/real/search_news?docid=70000021_9086a0d898b68852 May 20 2026; blog.csdn.net/2601_96073073/article/details/161245172 June 17 2026; so.html5.qq.com/page/real/search_news?docid=70000021_4876a101b0b78952 May 22 2026)
- **C-117** [P2] Google Antigravity 2.0 + Android CLI + AI code-migration agent (Google I/O May 20 2026) — Google I/O 2026 shipped Antigravity 2.0 (agentic web/mobile dev platform), Android CLI, AND a code-migration agent that auto-migrates legacy codebases (jQuery→React, Vue 2→Vue 3, ES5→ES2026, legacy build → Vite/Rollup). AI-DRIVEN-CODE-MIGRATION dimension distinct from C-104 (Codex CLI as QA tool — security constraint when using Codex ACP transport) because C-117 is the ENGINEERING-side use of an AI migration agent to refactor previously-working code — a fundamentally different risk class: the migration produces a NEW codebase whose behavior must be re-validated against the OLD codebase; distinct from C-113 (vibe coding AI-generated-code nondeterminism — AI generates NEW code from scratch) because C-117 covers AI-driven REFACTORING of existing legacy code whose full behavior is often undocumented, making regression-detection much harder. GameZipper's recurring 55-game rAF-cancelAnimationFrame template bug (v1.59.0) and BGM-setInterval leak bug (gamezipper-qa skill 2026-06-15) and 5+ games-data.js orphan-entry recurrences are EXACTLY the kind of latent bug an AI-migration pass would amplify by copying patterns from one file to many. Test: snapshot ALL games' behavior (golden screenshots, level-solvability proofs via IIFE-injection, full DOM diff) BEFORE invoking any AI migration agent; after migration, run snapshot-diff on EVERY game NOT just the migrated ones; specifically test for rAF-cancelAnimationFrame template, BGM-setInterval leaks, games-data.js orphan entries. (so.html5.qq.com/page/real/search_news?docid=70000021_9086a0d898b68852 May 20 2026; blog.csdn.net/hanzhixintianxia/article/details/161265277 June 4 2026; weibo.com/GoogleDevelopers May 12 2026)
- **W-178** [P3] Bank of America "agentic-phone era" analyst validation (June 11 2026 CaiLianShe / 财联社) — BoA published a post-WWDC26 analyst report explicitly framing iOS 27 / WWDC26 as the start of the 智能体手机 (agentic-phone) era. ANALYST-VALIDATED-AGENTIC-PHONE-INFLECTION-POINT dimension distinct from W-170 (2026 cybersecurity report — threat landscape: AI-Agent-impersonation + API-scale attacks + AI-browser/AI-phone "blackbox" risk) because W-178 is the MARKET-STRUCTURAL signal — a Tier-1 sell-side bank validating the agentic-phone era means QA budget allocation across the industry will tilt toward agentic-surface coverage; distinct from B-108 (iOS 27 Siri AI standalone app — single iOS feature) because W-178 is the analyst-validation signal that makes the feature strategically important; distinct from W-169 (Apple CEO transition Tim Cook → John Ternus — executive-leadership inflection) because W-178 is analyst-validation evidence. GameZipper QA roadmap must add "agentic-surface coverage" as a recurring line item; expect MORE agentic surfaces in 2026-2027 vendor releases than pre-WWDC26 plans suggested; track QA tooling vendors that support agentic-surface testing (Playwright TestAgents C-096, Razer Companion-AI C-107). (so.html5.qq.com/page/real/search_news?docid=70000021_1436a2aa8ad65652 June 11 2026 CaiLianShe)
- **B-111** [P2] iOS 27 Siri cross-app context search + iCloud conversation history (WWDC26 June 9 2026) — Siri AI in iOS 27 can "可以理解屏幕上的内容 可以结合个人上下文回答问题 可以跨 app 搜索信息、邮件、照片等内容" (understand screen content / combine with personal context / search across apps for mail, photos, etc). SIRI-CROSS-APP-CONTEXT-AWARE-ON-DEVICE-AI dimension distinct from B-108 (iOS 27 Siri AI standalone ChatGPT-style app — Siri as a new DISCOVERY surface) because B-111 covers Siri's CROSS-APP CONTEXT-MINING capability — Siri can read Mail, Photos, Messages, Notes and combine them with personal context to answer questions about whatever the user is currently viewing (including a GameZipper game page); distinct from P-071 (iOS 27 12GB RAM minimum — hardware gating) because B-111 is the PRIVACY surface not hardware gating; distinct from W-175 (iOS 27 Safari user-AI-generated extensions + Notify Me) because B-111 covers Siri's first-party context-awareness. GameZipper is exposed to indirect-AI-context-leak: a player mid-game can ask Siri to summarize the page or compare it to other games, and Siri will mine page DOM (potentially exposing ad-div contents, monetag-manager script URLs, debug logs) + player's Mail/Photos/Messages — a third party who can prompt-inject Siri via a malicious Monetag/AdSense creative could redirect Siri to mine player's private data. Test: on iOS 27 beta + stable ship, invoke Siri with "what's this page about?" and "what other games like this have I played?" and verify Siri's answer does NOT expose internal GameZipper implementation details; use aria-hidden on internal DOM; verify no prompt-injection patterns exist. (blog.csdn.net/aifengaopeng/article/details/161833067 June 9 2026; new.qq.com/rain/a/20260609A025RF00 June 9 2026)

## [v1.73.0] - 2026-06-19
### Added
- 6 new test cases from industry research (R193 Dynamic Test Intelligence cron)
- **S-142** [P1] AI-GENERATED-PATCH SUPPLY-CHAIN — AMD FFmpeg "AI slop" patches Jan 30 2026 maintainer rejection (FFmpeg publicly criticized AMD on official social-media account for submitting a pull request containing "AI-generated junk (AI slop)" commit messages for AMD's HIP SDK Windows-build support; the PR was eventually CLOSED). The AI-GENERATED-PATCH SUPPLY-CHAIN dimension distinct from S-124 (Glassworm invisible-Unicode source-text-level obfuscation — hides malicious logic in invisible Unicode characters) because S-142 hides a backdoor in AI-slop STYLING that exploits maintainer fatigue — an attacker submits an "AI-slop-looking" PR that maintainers rubber-stamp to clear their queue; distinct from S-141 (SANDWORM_MODE env-var-toggle runtime evasion) because S-142 is SOCIAL-ENGINEERING-of-maintainer-trust, not runtime-conditional logic; distinct from S-126 (eslint-config-prettier maintainer-phishing) because S-142 does NOT phish the maintainer — it submits code that LOOKS like benign AI-slop so the maintainer dismissively merges it. GameZipper depends on Phaser.js/Babylon.js/open-source libs accepting community PRs — as AI-slop PR volume grows, maintainer review quality degrades and a malicious PR may slip into a GameZipper dependency. (new.qq.com/rain/a/20260130A067F100 Jan 30 2026; so.html5.qq.com/page/real/search_news?docid=70000021_186697c803488452 Jan 30 2026)
- **S-143** [P2] AI-FLOODED-BUG-TRIAGE-QUEUE / AI-DISCLOSURE-DEADLINE-PRESSURE — Google overhauled Chrome bug-bounty program in 2026 to cope with the flood of AI-generated vulnerability reports (Chrome 149 record 429-CVE batch shipped June 2026) + Google Project Zero Big Sleep publicly shamed FFmpeg maintainers Nov 9 2025 to force rushed patch timelines + depthfirst security startup's autonomous agent scanned FFmpeg's ~1.5M lines of C and produced 21 confirmed zero-days at ~$1,000 each. The AI-FLOODED-BUG-TRIAGE-QUEUE / AI-DISCLOSURE-DEADLINE-PRESSURE dimension distinct from S-057 (20h exploit window SLA) because S-143 is the OPPOSITE direction — AI-discovered bugs are PUBLICLY EXPOSED forcing rushed patches that may introduce regressions, distinct from S-113 (Anthropic Mythos defensive discovery — responsible disclosure) and C-114 (Mythos offensive generation — capability) because S-143 is the SOC/bug-triage-DENIAL-OF-SERVICE dimension where AI-generated reports flood manual queues so real human CVEs get missed. GameZipper's Monetag/AdSense ad slots depend on browser security; rushed AI-disclosure-forced patches may regress canvas rendering. (thehackernews.com/search/label/Chrome June 6 2026; so.html5.qq.com/page/real/search_news?docid=70000021_5096910234518252 Nov 9 2025)
- **C-115** [P2] Meta 4× AI bug detection methodology April 22 2026 — Meta published a methodology for AI-assisted bug detection that improved the bug detection rate by 4× in their real codebase, COUNTER to the AI-generated-code-bypass (C-113 vibe-coding risk). The AI-ASSISTED-QA-METHODOLOGY dimension distinct from C-100/C-103 (Self-Healing Test Automation silent false-pass detection — locator-stability) because C-115 is a COVERAGE-INCREASE methodology not a locator-stability issue, distinct from C-098 (WebGPU "break on error" DevTools debug protocol — spec recommendation) because C-115 is a Meta-validated real-codebase result with quantified 4× improvement, distinct from C-093 (enterprise agentic AI playtesting Capcom/EA — gameplay testing) because C-115 covers CODE-LEVEL bug detection. GameZipper's recurring vibe-coding-QA-bypass bugs (rAF cancelAnimationFrame template error in 55 games, splash-screen dead-lock in 5+ games, missing input handlers, BGM setInterval leaks, games-data.js orphan entries recurring 5+ times) are EXACTLY what Meta's AI-assisted bug-detection methodology counters. (so.html5.qq.com/page/real/search_news?docid=70000021_40169e85c7b39652 April 22 2026)
- **W-174** [P3] METR randomized controlled trial — AI coding tools make experienced developers 19% SLOWER not faster (April 25 2026 retrospective on METR's 2025 RCT). METR conducted a randomized controlled trial where experienced open-source developers were given AI coding tools; the result: developers using AI tools took 19% LONGER to complete their assigned tasks. Crucially, the SUBJECTIVE PERCEPTION was the OPPOSITE — developers EXPECTED to be faster with AI before the trial, and BELIEVED they were faster after the trial, despite the objective 19% slowdown. The AI-CODING-PRODUCTIVITY-ILLUSION dimension distinct from C-113 (vibe-coding AI-generated-code nondeterminism — QUALITY risk) because W-174 is the QUANTITY/PRODUCTIVITY decision-basis dimension — GameZipper pipeline estimates based on "AI makes us 2× faster" are biased in the OPPOSITE direction, distinct from C-115 (Meta 4× AI bug detection — AI-as-QA-tool) because W-174 covers AI-as-coding-tool (may slow experienced devs down). GameZipper's recurring bugs are the understanding-debt failure mode; release planning assuming "Claude Code generates a game in 30 minutes" should apply a 1.19× METR-slowdown factor. (so.html5.qq.com/page/real/search_news?docid=70000021_56169ec6f4976052 April 25 2026)
- **W-175** [P2] iOS 27 Safari user-AI-generated extensions + Notify Me continuous webpage-monitoring (MacRumors June 12 2026 / new.qq.com June 13 2026) — iOS 27 Safari introduces TWO new game-relevant surfaces: (1) "Create Extension" — users describe a need in natural language and Apple Intelligence generates a custom Safari extension on-device (no App-Store review); (2) "Notify Me" — Safari continuously polls a webpage for content changes. The iOS-27-SAFARI-USER-AI-EXTENSION-AND-NOTIFY-ME-NEW-POLLING-SURFACE dimension distinct from W-129 (Safari 27 Apple Intelligence tab organization — tab reordering) because W-175 covers AI GENERATING new browser extensions on-device from a natural-language prompt (a CODE-EXECUTION dimension) AND a new periodic-polling load surface (a perf/cost dimension), distinct from S-128 (OpenClaw ClawHub AI-agent-marketplace — malicious skill distributed via marketplace) because W-175 covers BENIGN-NATURAL-LANGUAGE-PROMPT-generated extensions that may still be HARMFUL if the natural-language prompt is itself prompt-injected, distinct from W-173 (Chrome MV3 typosquatting window — malicious typosquatted clones in Chrome Web Store curated) because W-175 extensions are GENERATED ON-DEVICE BY APPLE-AI possibly UNREVIEWED by Apple. GameZipper game pages currently have no defense against user-generated Safari extensions that modify page DOM; Notify Me polling means a frequently-updating GameZipper game page generates N periodic HTTP pollers from iOS-Safari users. (new.qq.com/rain/a/20260613A02J4P00 June 13 2026; MacRumors June 12 2026)
- **P-071** [P2] iOS 27 12GB RAM minimum for advanced local AI features (WWDC26 June 9 2026) — Apple announced at WWDC26 that iOS 27's most advanced on-device AI features require 12GB+ RAM devices (only iPhone Air and a small subset of high-end iPhones meet this threshold). The gating is HARDWARE-LEVEL — iOS 27 silently DISABLES the advanced AI features on <12GB devices with NO ERROR MESSAGE. The iOS-RAM-TIER-DIVIDE-FOR-AI-FEATURES dimension distinct from P-048 (entry-tier Mali-G57/Adreno Android GPU baseline — graphics performance) because P-071 is the iOS-RAM dimension specifically for AI workloads, distinct from B-107 (Android 17 memory-pressure enforcement — Android platform behavior) because P-071 is Apple-platform AI-FEATURE GATING based on hardware capability, distinct from B-108 (iOS 27 Siri AI standalone app — Siri as a new discovery surface) because P-071 covers which iOS devices can RUN the advanced Siri/local-AI features at all. GameZipper's FUTURE AI features (NPC dialogue via WebLLM, voice-driven game commands via Web Speech API + on-device ASR, image generation via WebGPU LLM inference) will silently fail/degrade on iOS-27 iPhones with <12GB RAM — the SILENT disablement is a GameZipper-customer-support hazard. (so.html5.qq.com/page/real/search_news?docid=70000021_5106a275b0d01252 June 9 2026 DoNews)
